0                                   6310              *
                                    6311              **
                                    6312              **  WYLBUR SCANNER DOCUMENTATION
                                    6313              **
                                    6314              **  AS OF 11/89 WYLBURS OLD SCANNER IS BEING REPLACED BY A
                                    6315              **  NEW SCANNER.  THE FOLLOWING COMMENTS REFER TO THE NEW
                                    6316              **  SCANNER.  THIS DOCUMENTATION IS NOT COMPLETE, BUT REMEMBER !
                                    6317              **
                                    6318              **  "SOME IS BETTER THAN NONE."
                                    6319              **
                                    6320              **  HISTORICAL NOTE (11/89):
                                    6321              **  THE NSCAN AND NKW PREFIX REFER TO 'NEW' SCAN AND 'NEW'
                                    6322              **  KEYWORD ENTRY DSECT.  AS TIME GOES ON 'NEW' WILL BECOME
                                    6323              **  THE REGULAR.  CHANCES ARE THAT THE 'N' PART OF MANY
                                    6324              **  NAMES (IE. NSCAN) WILL REMAIN. OH WELL.
                                    6325              **
                                    6326              **  -------------------------------------------------
                                    6327              **
                                    6328              **  DOCUMENTATION OUTLINE
                                    6329              **
                                    6330              **  1. MACRO INTERFACE
                                    6331              **  2. SCAN CONTROL BLOCK
                                    6332              **  3. ROUTINES INTERFACES
                                    6333              **     (FOR SCAN ROUTINE, MATCH ROUTINE, PROCESSING ROUTINE)
                                    6334              **
                                    6335              **  -------------------------------------------------
                                    6336              **
                                    6337              **
                                    6338              **  MACRO INTERFACE:
                                    6339              **
                                    6340              **  THESE MACROS ARE NOT FULLY DOCUMENTED.  SEE WYLBUR CODE
                                    6341              **  FOR EXAMPLES, AND ACTUAL MACROS FOR DETAILS.
                                    6342              **
                                    6343              **  SET UP SCAN CONTROL BLOCK ..
                                    6344              **    SCINIT - SET UP STRING LOC,LEN TO SCAN
                                    6345              **    SETSKIP - SET UP SCAN SKIP TABLE
                                    6346              **    SETSTOP - SET UP SCAN STOP TABLE
                                    6347              **    SETSCKWS - SET UP SCAN SCKWS TABLE ADDRESS
                                    6348              **
                                    6349              **  CALL SCAN ..
                                    6350              **    SCAN - CALL SCANNER
                                    6351              **    SCANCHK - CHECK/WRITE ANY SCAN ERRORS
                                    6352              **
                                    6353              **  TO PROCESS SCANNED TOKEN(S) ..
                                    6354              **    SCTOK - RETURN LOC,LEN OF CURRENT TOKEN
                                    6355              **    SCUPTOK - POINT RX TO UPPER CASE BLANK PADDED TOKEN
                                    6356              **    SCULTOK - POINT RX TO UPLOW CASE BLANK PADDED TOKEN
                                    6357              **    SCDQUOTE - DEQUOTE TOKEN INTO SPECIFIED AREA B/PADDED
                                    6358              **    SCUPCASE - UPPER CASE TOKEN INTO SPECIFIED AREA B/PADDED
                                    6359              **
                                    6360              **  SET KEYWORD TABLE ENTRY
                                    6361              **    SCKW <KEYWORD STRING>,<ROUTINE>,<MATCH INFO,FLAGS>,PARM1,PARM2
                                    6362              **
                                    6363              **  TO SAVE/RESTOR SCAN CONTROL BLOCKS OR PORTIONS..

0                                   6364              **    SCPUSH - SAVE COPY OF SCAN CB ON STACK
                                    6365              **    SCPOP - RESTORE SAVED SCAN CB
                                    6366              **    SCCLR - CLEAR CURRENT SCAN CB
                                    6367              **    SCSAVE - SAVE COPY OF SCAN CB IN SPECIFIC AREA
                                    6368              **    SCRSTR - RESTOR COPY OF SCAN CB FROM SPECIFIC AREA
                                    6369              **
                                    6370              **
                                    6371              **  TO GET SCAN CONTROL BLOCK ADDRESSABILITY ...
                                    6372              **    SCCBADR <RX> - PUT ADDR OF SCAN CB IN RX
                                    6373              **
                                    6374              **
                                    6375              **  MISC SCAN MACROS ...
                                    6376              **    SCANSTR - SAME AS SCAN BUT W/SKIP=' ' STOP=' ,;='
                                    6377              **    SCINFO - RETURN CURRENT REMAINDER TO SCAN LOC AND LEN
                                    6378              **    SCBKUP - BACKUP BY LAST TOKEN
                                    6379              **        (CAN ONLY BE USED FOR LAST TOKEN SCANNED)
                                    6380              **    SCSEG - SEG AN ERROR TO SCAN CB
                                    6381              **    SCSEGCLR - CLEAR ERR MSG IN SCAN CB
                                    6382              **
                                    6383              **  PUSH ROUTINE MACRO ..
                                    6384              **    PUSHRTN - USED FOR PUSHED SCKWS(RECURSIVE KW LOOKUP)
                                    6385              **    XPUSHRTN -USED FOR PUSHED SCKWS (RECURSIVE KW LOOKUP)
                                    6386              **
                                    6387              **  MORE DETAILED COMMENTS:
                                    6388              **
                                    6389              **
                                    6390              **  SET UP SCAN CONTROL BLOCK ..
                                    6391              **    SCINIT - SET UP STRING LOC,LEN TO SCAN
                                    6392              **    SETSKIP - SET UP SCAN SKIP TABLE
                                    6393              **    SETSTOP - SET UP SCAN STOP TABLE
                                    6394              **    SETSCKWS - SET UP SCAN SCKWS TABLE ADDRESS
                                    6395              **  THESE MACROS SET UP THE SCAN ENVIRONMENT. ONLY SCINIT
                                    6396              **  IS REQUIRED. SETSKIP AND SETSTOP CAN BE USED TO RESET
                                    6397              **  THE SKIP AND STOP TABLES USED WHEN SCANNING.  TO SEE
                                    6398              **  HOW SKIP/STOP CHARS ARE SPECIFIED LOOK IN 'EXTENDED
                                    6399              **  EXEC' DOCUMENT UNDER 'SYSCALL SCAN'. THE CALLS WORK IN
                                    6400              **  THE SAME MANNER. SETSCKWS WILL SET THE ADDRESS OF THE
                                    6401              **  SCAN TABLES USED.  THE DEFAULTS FOR SET/SKIP ARE TO
                                    6402              **  USE WYLBURS WIERD CONVENTIONS. THE DEFAULT SCKWS ARE NONE.
                                    6403              **
                                    6404              **
                                    6405              **  CALL SCAN ..
                                    6406              **    SCAN - CALL SCANNER
                                    6407              **    SCANCHK - CHECK/WRITE ANY SCAN ERRORS
                                    6408              **  THE SCAN MACRO CALLS THE SCAN ROUTINE, SEE DOCUMENTATION ON
                                    6409              **  THE SCAN ROUTINE INTERFACE BELOW.  ALL INPUTS TO SCAN ARE
                                    6410              **  PASSED IN THE SCAN CONTROL BLOCK.  THESE ARE SET UP WITH
                                    6411              **  THE SCINIT, SETSKIP, SETSTOP, AND SETSCKW MACROS.  TYPICALLY
                                    6412              **  THE SETSKIP, SETSTOP AND SETSCKW MACROS ARE NOT USED AND
                                    6413              **  ARE DEFAULTED.  AN SCINIT MUST BE DONE. BUT IS USUALLY DONE
                                    6414              **  ONCE AT THE START OF EACH COMMAND IN THE COMM MODULE.
                                    6415              **  THE TYPICAL USE OF THE 'SCAN' MACRO WILL DEFAULT THE SKIP
                                    6416              **  START TABLES.  MORE UNUSUAL WAYS TO HANDLE THE SCANNING
                                    6417              **  INPUT PARAMETERS ARE COMMENTED ON IN THE ACTUAL 'SCAN'
1SCAN     (SCAN2025) (12:54) (15MAR04) WYLBUR SCAN ROUTINES                                                                 Page    7
0Current Usings:  (CP,R11) (CV,R12)

+___    ______ ____    _____ _____  ____ __ ______    ______ _________
0                                   6418              **  MACRO.
                                    6419              **  THE SCANCHK MACRO, WILL DETECT AND PROCESS ANY SCAN ERRORS
                                    6420              **  FOUND.  IF THERE IS AN ERROR, CONTROL WILL NOT RETURN AFTER
                                    6421              **  A SCANCHK MACRO IS ISSUED.
                                    6422              **
                                    6423              **
                                    6424              **  TO PROCESS SCANNED TOKEN(S) ..
                                    6425              **    SCTOK - RETURN LOC,LEN OF CURRENT TOKEN
                                    6426              **    SCUPTOK - POINT RX TO UPPER CASE BLANK PADDED TOKEN
                                    6427              **    SCULTOK - POINT RX TO UPLOW CASE BLANK PADDED TOKEN
                                    6428              **    SCDQUOTE - DEQUOTE TOKEN INTO SPECIFIED AREA B/PADDED
                                    6429              **    SCUPCASE - UPPER CASE TOKEN INTO SPECIFIED AREA B/PADDED
                                    6430              **  SCUPTOK, SCULTOK POINT A REGISTER TO A 16 BYTE AREA, SO BE
                                    6431              **  CAREFUL IF TOKEN SCANNED IS LARGER.  SCDQUOTE DOES DEQUOTE
                                    6432              **  STRING INTO AN AREA. IF STRING IS NOT QUOTED IT WILL UPPER
                                    6433              **  CASE STRING INTO AREA.  R1,R0 ARE DEQUOTED STRING LOC,LEN.
                                    6434              **  SCUPCASE WILL UPPER CASE STRING INTO AREA. R1,R0 ARE UPPER
                                    6435              **  CASED STRING LOCATION AND LENGTH.
                                    6436              **
                                    6437              **  SET KEYWORD TABLE ENTRY
                                    6438              **    SCKW <KEYWORD STRING>,<ROUTINE>,<MATCH INFO,FLAGS>,PARM1,PARM2
                                    6439              **  SEE MANY EXAMPLES OF SCKW IN CODE.  THIS MACRO GENERATES A
                                    6440              **  PROPERLY FILLED OUT NKW (NEW KEYWORD CONTROL BLOCK). SO CHECK
                                    6441              **  OUT THE NKW DESECT FOR MORE INFO.
                                    6442              **
                                    6443              **  TO SAVE/RESTOR SCAN CONTROL BLOCKS OR PORTIONS..
                                    6444              **    SCPUSH - SAVE COPY OF SCAN CB ON STACK
                                    6445              **    SCPOP - RESTORE SAVED SCAN CB
                                    6446              **    SCCLR - CLEAR CURRENT SCAN CB
                                    6447              **    SCSAVE - SAVE COPY OF SCAN CB IN SPECIFIC AREA
                                    6448              **    SCRSTR - RESTOR COPY OF SCAN CB FROM SPECIFIC AREA
                                    6449              **  SCPUSH, SCPOP MUST USE STANDARD STACK DISCIPLINE.
                                    6450              **  SCSAVE AND SCRSTR CAN BE POINTED TO ANY AREA.
                                    6451              **
                                    6452              **  TO GET SCAN CONTROL BLOCK ADDRESSABILITY ...
                                    6453              **    SCCBADR <RX> - PUT ADDR OF SCAN CB IN RX
                                    6454              **  THE SCAN CONTROL BLOCK IS IN THE CP AND IS POINTED TO
                                    6455              **  BY CPSCANP.  MACROS ASSUME THIS IS TRUE.  THE SCCBADR
                                    6456              **  LOADS THE ADDRESS FROM CPSCANP.  IF YOU WANT TO USE THE
                                    6457              **  SCANNER IN A NOT-CP ENVIRONMENT, IT IS POSSIBLE IF YOU
                                    6458              **  CHANGE THE LOCATION AND THE WAY THAT THE CONTROL BLOCK
                                    6459              **  LOCATION IS FOUND.  (IE. CHANGE THE SCCBADDR MACRO!.)
                                    6460              **  THE SCAN CODE ITSELF DOES NOT USE THE CP. (VERIFY !!)
                                    6461              **  NOR DOES IT HAVE ANY KNOWLEDGE OF CPSCANP. (VERIFY !!)
                                    6462              **
                                    6463              **
                                    6464              **  MISC SCAN MACROS ...
                                    6465              **    SCANSTR - SAME AS SCAN BUT W/SKIP=' ' STOP=' ,;='
                                    6466              **    SCINFO - RETURN CURRENT REMAINDER TO SCAN LOC AND LEN
                                    6467              **    SCBKUP - BACKUP BY LAST TOKEN
                                    6468              **        (CAN ONLY BE USED FOR LAST TOKEN SCANNED)
                                    6469              **    SCSEG - SEG AN ERROR TO SCAN CB
                                    6470              **    SCSEGCLR - CLEAR ERR MSG IN SCAN CB
                                    6471              **  SCANSTR IS IDENTICAL TO SCAN MACRO EXCEPT THAT IT USES

+___    ______ ____    _____ _____  ____ __ ______    ______ _________
0                                   6472              **  DIFFERENT SKIP/STOP TABLES.  SKIP=' ' STOP=' ,;='.
                                    6473              **  SCSEG, SCSEGCLR ARE USED TO RETURN SCAN ERRORS BY THE
                                    6474              **  TOKEN PROCESSING ROUTINES.  (IN ACTUALITY, MOST JUST
                                    6475              **  EXIT DIRECTLY TO CVERROR)
                                    6476              **
                                    6477              **  PUSH ROUTINE MACRO ..
                                    6478              **    PUSHRTN - USED FOR PUSHED SCKWS(RECURSIVE KW LOOKUP)
                                    6479              **    XPUSHRTN -USED FOR PUSHED SCKWS (RECURSIVE KW LOOKUP)
                                    6480              **  THESE MACROS IMPLEMENT RECURSIVE KW LOOKUP OF PUSHED
                                    6481              **  KEYWORD TABLES.  YOU HAVE TO LOOK AT SCAN CODE TO SEE
                                    6482              **  WHAT IS GOING ON. OR JUST USE THE MACRO BLINDLY BY
                                    6483              **  EXAMPLE.
                                    6484              **
                                    6485              **  OTHER COMMENTS:
                                    6486              **
                                    6487              **  ALL FIELDS IN THE CONTROL BLOCK MAY BE MODIFIED BY THE
                                    6488              **  KNOWLEDGEABLE PROGRAMMER.  TO INITIALIZE THE CONTROL BLOCK
                                    6489              **  THE MACROS: SCINIT, SETSKIP, SETSTOP MACROS ARE PROVIEDED.
                                    6490              **  THEY ALL EXPECT A STRING LOCATION AND LENGTH AS ARGUMENTS.
                                    6491              **
                                    6492              **  THE SCAN MACRO CALLS THE SCAN ROUTINE. A KEYWORD TABLE IS
                                    6493              **  OPTIONAL.   TO SPECIFY A KEWORD TABLE, THE NAME MUST BE
                                    6494              **  SPECIFIED ON THE NSCAN MACRO.  ALSO SPECIFY ONLY THE NAME
                                    6495              **  NOT HOW IT IS TO BE LOADED (EG. LA: L: LH:). THIS IS FOR
                                    6496              **  *-CODE COMPATIBILITY.
                                    6497              **
                                    6498              **  NOTE: ALL MACROS ASSUME THAT CPNSCANP POINTS TO VALID
                                    6499              **  SCAN CONTROL BLOCK.  TO USE IT IN NON-CP ADDRESSABLE STATE
                                    6500              **  MOST MACROS WILL HAVE TO BE BYPASSED.  THE SCAN MACRO
                                    6501              **  WILL CHANGE R14-R2.
                                    6502              **
                                    6503              **
                                    6504              **  -----------------------------------------------------------
                                    6505              **
                                    6506              **  SCAN CONTROL BLOCK
                                    6507              **
                                    6508              **  TO FULLY UNDERSTAND THE SCAN ROUTINES, YOU NEED TO LOOK AT
                                    6509              **  THE SCAN CONTROL BLOCK.  ALSO TO FIGURE OUT THE NKW MACRO
                                    6510              **  FOR CODING KEYWORD TABLE ENTRIES, CHECK OUT THE 'NKW' DSECT.
                                    6511              **
                                    6512              **
                                    6513              ** ------------------------------------------------------------
                                    6514              **
                                    6515              **  ROUTINE INTERFACES (VERIFY W/COMMENTS IN ACTUAL CODE !!)
                                    6516              **
                                    6517              **
                                    6518              **  SCAN ROUTINE:
                                    6519              **
                                    6520              **  ON ENTRY:
                                    6521              **    R1 - POINTS TO SCAN CONTROL BLOCK
                                    6522              **    THE SCAN CONTROL BLOCK INPUT PARAMETERS ARE:
                                    6523              **      STRING LOCATION, LENGTH; THESE ARE UPDATED TO REFLECT
                                    6524              **         REMAINING STRING TO SCAN.
                                    6525              **      ADDRESS OF SKIP AND STOP TRT TABLES (ZERO TO USE DEFAULT).
1SCAN     (SCAN2025) (12:54) (15MAR04) WYLBUR SCAN ROUTINES                                                                 Page    9
0Current Usings:  (CP,R11) (CV,R12)
0Loc    Object Code    Addr1 Addr2  Stmt Lv Lineno    Source Statement           (Hibal 5, Asmedit 3.3)  HLASM R4.0  2004/03/15 12.54
+___    ______ ____    _____ _____  ____ __ ______    ______ _________
0                                   6526              **      ADDRESS OF KEYWORD TABLE (ZERO IF NONE).
                                    6527              **      SCAN CONTROL FLAGS. (ONLY BLANK TOKEN FLAG ALLOWED SO FAR).
                                    6528              **
                                    6529              **  ON EXIT:
                                    6530              **    R1,R0 - LOC, LEN OF LAST TOKEN/PARM SCANNED
                                    6531              **    R15 - ZERO IF NO ERROR
                                    6532              **    R15 - NZ, IF ERROR
                                    6533              **
                                    6534              **    THE SCAN CONTROL BLOCK IS UPDATED AS FOLLOWS:
                                    6535              **    THE STRING LOC, LEN POINTERS ARE UPDATED TO POINT TO THE
                                    6536              **      REMAINDER OF THE STRING
                                    6537              **    THE TOKEN LOC, LEN POINTERS POINT TO THE LAST TOKEN OR
                                    6538              **      PARAMETER SCANNED.
                                    6539              **    THE TOKEN TYPE FLAGS ARE SET, AND IF NUMBER OR LINENUMBER TYPE
                                    6540              **      THEN THE TOKEN VALUE IS SET.
                                    6541              **    THE TOKEN (IF NO ERROR) ALSO PLACED LEFT JUSTIFIED BLANK
                                    6542              **      PADDED IN BOTH UPPER AND UPLOW CASE WITHIN THE SCAN CB.
                                    6543              **
                                    6544              **  REGISTER USAGE:
                                    6545              **    R2 - SCAN CB
                                    6546              **
                                    6547              **    R2 IS USED INTERNALLY WITHIN THIS MODULE TO POINT AT THE
                                    6548              **    SCAN CONTROL BLOCK.  IT IS ALSO PASSED (IN R2) TO THE
                                    6549              **    MATCH AND PROCESSING ROUTINES.
                                    6550              **
                                    6551              **
                                    6552              **  COMMENTS:
                                    6553              **  IF NO KEYWORD TABLE IS SPECIFIED:
                                    6554              **  ONLY ONE TOKEN IS SCANNED, IT'S TYPE IS DETERMINED.  IF IT'S
                                    6555              **  TYPE IS NUMBER (INTEGER) OR LINE NO, THEN ITS VALUE IS RETURNED
                                    6556              **  IN THE SCAN CONTROL BLOCK.  THE TOKEN IS PLACED LEFT JUSTIFIED
                                    6557              **  BLANK PADDED IN UPPER AND UPLOW CASE WITHIN THE SCAN CB.
                                    6558              **  THE ONLY ERROR THAT CAN OCCUR IS 'MISMATCHED QUOTE OR
                                    6559              **  PARENTHESIS'
                                    6560              **
                                    6561              **  IF A KEYWORD TABLE IS SPECIFIED:
                                    6562              **  A TOKEN IS SCANNED AS ABOVE.  THIS TOKEN IS COMPARED AGAINST ALL
                                    6563              **  THE ENTRIES IN THE KEYWORD TABLE.  IF A MATCH IS FOUND THE
                                    6564              **  KEYWORD ROUTINE IS CALLED.  UPON RETURN FROM THE KEYWORD ROUTINE
                                    6565              **  ANOTHER TOKEN IS SCANNED.  THIS TOKEN IS COMPARED AGAINST ALL
                                    6566              **  ENTRIES IN THE KEYWORD TABLE.  IF A MATCH IS FOUND, THE MATCHING
                                    6567              **  KEYWORD ROUTINE IS CALLED.  ... AND SO ON ...
                                    6568              **  THIS CONTINUES UNTIL:  (A) ALL TOKENS IN THE STRING ARE SCANNED
                                    6569              **  (B) NO MATCH IS FOUND, (C) THE KEYWORD ROUTINE RETURNS A NON-ZERO
                                    6570              **  RETURN CODE, OR (D) AN ERROR OCCURS DURING THE SCAN.
                                    6571              **
                                    6572              **  WE EXAMINE EACH CASE:
                                    6573              **    (A) ALL TOKENS IN STRING ARE SCANNED:  THE NORMAL CASE.
                                    6574              **    (B) NO MATCH IS FOUND:  THIS IS NOT AN ERROR CONDITION.
                                    6575              **          TYPICALLY THIS DOES NOT HAPPEN AS THERE IS A CATCH-ALL
                                    6576              **          KEYWORD ENTRY, THAT WILL GENERATE AN ERROR.
                                    6577              **    (C) IF THE KEYWORD ROUTINE RETURNS A NON-ZERO IN R15, THE
                                    6578              **        SCAN WILL BE STOPPED, AND R15 WILL BE RETURNED TO THE
                                    6579              **        SCAN CALLER.
1SCAN     (SCAN2025) (12:54) (15MAR04) WYLBUR SCAN ROUTINES                                                                 Page   10
0Current Usings:  (CP,R11) (CV,R12)
0Loc    Object Code    Addr1 Addr2  Stmt Lv Lineno    Source Statement           (Hibal 5, Asmedit 3.3)  HLASM R4.0  2004/03/15 12.54
+___    ______ ____    _____ _____  ____ __ ______    ______ _________
0                                   6580              **    (D) THE ONLY ERRORS ENCOUNTERED DURING THE SCAN ARE
                                    6581              **        (1) MISMATCHED QUOTES OR PARENTHESIS, OR
                                    6582              **        (2) THE MATCH ROUTINE DETECTS AN ERROR, EG.
                                    6583              **            THE MATCH ROUTINE EXPECTS A PARM, BUT THERE IS NOT
                                    6584              **            ONE OR THE PARM IS INVALID TYPE OR VALUE
                                    6585              **
                                    6586              **  ------
                                    6587              **
                                    6588              **  EACH MATCH ROUTINE IS CALLED AS FOLLOWS:
                                    6589              **  ON ENTRY:
                                    6590              **     R15 - ZERO
                                    6591              **     R0 - NOT USED
                                    6592              **     R1 - NKW (KEYWORD (SCKW) INFO BLOCK)
                                    6593              **     R2 - SCAN CONTROL BLOCK
                                    6594              **     R3-R6 SAME AS ON ENTRY TO NSCAN ROUTINE
                                    6595              **
                                    6596              **  ON EXIT:
                                    6597              **     R15 - NEGATIVE, ERROR (PLACE ERROR MSG IN NSCNCB)
                                    6598              **     R15 - ZERO, MATCH FOUND
                                    6599              **     R15 - POSITIVE, MATCH NOT FOUND
                                    6600              **     R0-R1 - VALUE TO PASS TO KEYWORD ROUTINE (IF R15 ZERO)
                                    6601              **             (PRETURN MUST BE USED TO CHANGE THESE VALUES.)
                                    6602              **     R2-R6 - DO NOT CHANGE
                                    6603              **
                                    6604              **  NOTE: IF YOU WANT A MATCH ROUTINE TO DO A LOT OF RESCANNING
                                    6605              **  ETC, YOU MUST BE AWARE THAT YOU WILL BE MAKING CHANGES TO
                                    6606              **  THE SCAN CONTROL BLOCK (NSCNCB).  AND YOU MUST BE SURE THAT
                                    6607              **  THE CHANGES ARE COOL VIS-A-VIS THE SCAN CALLS THAT FOLLOW.
                                    6608              **  BE COOL
                                    6609              **
                                    6610              **  ------
                                    6611              **
                                    6612              **  EACH KEYWORD ROUTINE IS CALLED AS FOLLOWS:
                                    6613              **  ON ENTRY:
                                    6614              **     R15 - ZERO
                                    6615              **     R1,R0 - AS SUPPLIED BY THE MATCH ROUTINE, TYPICALLY ..
                                    6616              **             R1,R0 - LOC, LEN OF KEYWORD/PARM FOR STRINGS
                                    6617              **             R0 - VALUE FOR INTEGERS VALUEx1000 FOR LINE NUMBERS
                                    6618              **             SEE COMMENTS AT SPECIFIC MATCH ROUTINE
                                    6619              **     R2 - SCAN CONTROL BLOCK
                                    6620              **     R3-R6 SAME AS ON ENTRY TO NSCAN ROUTINE
                                    6621              **
                                    6622              **  ON EXIT:
                                    6623              **     R15 - ZERO, CONTINUE SCAN
                                    6624              **     R15 - NON-ZERO, STOP SCAN  (R15 VAL RETURNED TO NSCAN CALLER)
                                    6625              **     R0-R2 - DO NOT CHANGE
                                    6626              **     R3-R6 - PASSED BACK TO CALLER OF SCAN ROUTINE.
                                    6627              **             (PRETURN MUST BE USED TO CHANGE THESE VALUES.)
                                    6628              **
                                    6629              **  NOTE:
                                    6630              **  ALL KEYWORD ROUTINES SHOULD USE THE STANDARD XPROC/PROC/PEND
                                    6631              **  INTERFACE. THEY ARE RESPONSIBLE FOR RESTORING ALL REGISTERS
                                    6632              **  USED.  THEY SHOULD ALWAYS RETURN TO THE CALLER.  THIS GIVES
                                    6633              **  THE NSCAN CALLER CONTROL!

0                                   6634              **
                                    6635              **  -----
                                    6636              **
                                    6637              **  KEYWORD ENTRIES AND MATCHES:
                                    6638              **
                                    6639              **  MATCH ROUTINES CAN DO WHAT THEY WANT, BUT IN GENERAL:
                                    6640              **  KEYWORD ENTRIES CAN MATCH TOKENS, NUMBERS, LINE NUMBERS, OR
                                    6641              **  ANYTHING.  THE FIRST KEYWORD ENTRY THAT MATCHES WILL BE CALLED.
                                    6642              **  KEYWORD ENTRIES CAN SPECIFY THAT A CERTAIN TYPE OF PARAMETER
                                    6643              **  BE SCANNED.  IF A PARAMETER IS SCANNED, IT (AND NOT THE TOKEN)
                                    6644              **  WILL BE CONTAINED IN THE SCAN CONTROL BLOCK.  IF A PARAMETER
                                    6645              **  SCAN IS REQUESTED AND THE PARM IS MISSING OR NOT OF THE
                                    6646              **  SPECIFIED TYPE AN ERROR OCCURS.
                                    6647              **
                                    6648              **
                                    6649              **  -----
                                    6650              **
                                    6651              **  ERRORS:
                                    6652              **  ERRORS RETURN NON-ZERO RETURN CODE IN R15.  ALSO FOR SCANNER
                                    6653              **  GENERATED ERRORS (NEG RETURN CODE) AN ERROR MESSAGE IS
                                    6654              **  PLACED IN THE SCAN CONTROL BLOCK.  IF A KEYWORD ROUTINE
                                    6655              **  GENERATES A NON-ZERO RETURN CODE, THAT ROUTINE IS RESPONSIBLE
                                    6656              **  FOR EITHER SEG'ING AN ERROR MSG, PUTTING AN ERROR MSG IN THE
                                    6657              **  SCAN CONTROL BLOCK, OR DOING NOTHING.
                                    6658              **
                                    6659              **  TYPICALLY, A CATCH-ALL KEYWORD ENTRY IS SPECIFIED AT THE END
                                    6660              **  OF THE KEYWORD LIST TO CATCH INVALID KEYWORDS.  MOST ERROR
                                    6661              **  RETURNED BY THE SCANNER ARE DUE TO MISSING OR BAD PARMS.
                                    6662              **  IF YOU NEED MORE CONTROL OVER THE DETECTION AND PROCESSING
                                    6663              **  OF ERRORS, YOU MAY WANT TO SCAN THE PARMS YOURSELF. IT IS
                                    6664              **  NOT DIFFICULT, BUT RARELY NECESSARY.
                                    6665              **
                                    6666              **  ------
                                    6667              **
                                    6668              *

0                                   6837              *
                                    6838              **
                                    6839              **  SCAN
                                    6840              **
                                    6841              **  ON ENTRY:
                                    6842              **    R1 - SCAN CONTROL BLOCK
                                    6843              **
                                    6844              **  ON EXIT:
                                    6845              **    R1,R0 - LOC LENGTH OF LAST SCANNED ITEM/PARM
                                    6846              **    R15 - ZERO, IF SCAN OK
                                    6847              **    R15 - MINUS, IF SCAN ERROR, ERR MSG PLACED IN SCAN CB
                                    6848              **    R15 - POSITIVE, USER RETURN, SET BY KEYWORD ROUTINE.
                                    6849              **    R2 - SCAN CB,  ALL TOKEN, STRING STUFF UPDATED.
                                    6850              **
                                    6851              **
                                    6852              **  REGISTER USAGE:
                                    6853              **    R2 - SCAN CB        (INTERNAL TO SCAN MODULE)
                                    6854              **
                                    6855              **  NOTE:
                                    6856              **  IF KW TABLE IS SUPPLIED, ,,, WE LOOP THRU EACH TOKEN
                                    6857              **  CALLING THE APROPRIATE KEYWORD ROUTINES.
                                    6858              **
                                    6859              **  NOTE2: !!!
                                    6860              **  WHEN CALLING THE MATCH/PROCESSING ROUTINES,  REGISTERS
                                    6861              **  ARE SET BY POINTING DIRECTLY INTO THE STACK. THIS IS
                                    6862              **  HIGHLY NON-STANDARD !!
                                    6863              **
                                    6864              **  IMPLEMENTATION NOTE:
                                    6865              **  MOST ROUTINE PARAMETERS ARE PASSED IN THE SCAN CONTROL
                                    6866              **  BLOCK.  CHECK IT OUT.
                                    6867              **
                                    6868              **  SEE COMMENTS AT START OF MODULE.
                                    6869              **  SEE COMMENTS AT START OF MODULE.  !!!!
                                    6870              **
                                    6871              *

                                    7478              **  WILL ONLY FIND THE FIRST MATCH.

                                    7845              **    R15 - NON ZERO, IF NO MATCH

                                    7853              **  USER INTERFACE.

                                    7856              **  THERE ARE SOME (MANY) DIFFICULTIES SETTING UP THE REGISTERS
                                    7857              **  FOR THE CALL TO USERS ROUTINE.  THERE IS MUCH REGISTER
                                    7858              **  JUGGLING... THE BIGGEST TRICKS ARE: (A.) THAT R14 MUST POINT
                                    7859              **  TO THE KEYWORD TABLE ENTRY... SO WE CAN USE IT TO GET THE
                                    7860              **  ROUTINE ADDRESS AFTER ALL THE OTHER REGS ARE SET UP.
                                    7861              **  AND (B.) THAT WE MUST POINT INTO THE STACK TO RECOVER
                                    7862              **  REGS AT THE TIME OF THE CALL TO SCAN.  AND ALSO TO POINT
                                    7863              **  TO USERS WORK AREA AT THE TIME OF THE CALL TO SCAN.

                                    8518              **
                                    8519              **  ON ENTRY:

                                    8522              **    NSCNLEN - STRING LEN

0                                   9132              *
                                    9133              **
                                    9134              **  SETTYPE - DETERMINE TYPE
                                    9135              **
                                    9136              **  ON ENTRY:
                                    9137              **    R15 - ZERO, IF SCAN OK;  NEG, IF SCAN ERROR
                                    9138              **    SCAN CB - TOKEN LOC, LEN;
                                    9139              **
                                    9140              **  ON EXIT:
                                    9141              **    R15 - SAME AS ENTRY VALUE, ALSO
                                    9142              **    SET TYPE FLAGS AS FOLLOWS, (VALUE SET FOR NUM, LNO TYPES):
                                    9143              **       NULL - TOKEN LEN 0
                                    9144              **       LNO - LINE NUMBER (CONTAINS DECIMAL, VAL IS x1000)
                                    9145              **             (EG. 123.2  12. .123 12.2222222)
                                    9146              **             (NOTE: LONG DECIMALS TRUNCATED TO 3 PLACES)
                                    9147              **       NUM - INTEGER NUMBER (MAY BE NEG)
                                    9148              **             (EG. -123 +123 12)
                                    9149              **       ERR - IF R15 NEG ON ENTRY
                                    9150              **       TOKEN - ANY OTHER
                                    9151              **
                                    9152              **
                                    9153              **  NOTE:
                                    9154              **  NO ERRORS ARE DETECTED BY THIS ROUTINE.  NUMBERS ARE CHECKED
                                    9155              **  ONLY FOR MAX SIZE.  IF NUMBERS ARE INVALID, THEY WILL BE
                                    9156              **  TREATED AS TOKENS.  IF R15 IS NZ, THEN THE TYPE FLAG IS SET
                                    9157              **  TO ERROR.  THAT IS IT.
                                    9158              **
                                    9159              *

 000000 00                          9168  1           SETTFLG    FLAG

 SETTFLG.SETTDEC   40 ONES          9177  1                      FLAG  SETTDEC             DECIMAL ENCOUNTERED

                                   22565                                                                                   
                                   22566                XSCANSTR - SCAN STRING                                             
                                   22567                                                                                   
                                   22568                ON ENTRY:                                                          
                                   22569                     R0 - LENGTH OF STRING TO SCAN                                 
                                   22570                     R1 - LOCATION OF STRING TO SCAN                               
                                   22571                     R2 - LOCATION OF SKIP STRING                                  
                                   22572                     R3 - LENGTH OF SKIP STRING                                    
                                   22573                     R4 - LOCATION OF STOP STRING                                  
                                   22574                     R5 - LENGTH OF STOP STRING                                    
                                   22575                                                                                   
                                   22576                ON EXIT:                                                           
                                   22577                     R0 - TOKEN LENGTH                                             
                                   22578                     R1 - TOKEN LOCATION                                           
                                   22579                     R2 - REMAINING STRING LOCATION                                
                                   22580                     R3 - REMAINING STRING LENGTH                                  
                                   22581                     R4 - TYPE STRING LOCATION                                     
                                   22582                     R5 - TYPE STRING LENGTH                                       
                                   22583                    R15 - CC=ZERO                                                  
                                   22584                                                                                   
                                   22585                SEE SYSCALL SCAN DOCUMENTATION FOR DETAILS.                        
                                   22586                SEE SYSCALL SCAN_PARM DOCUMENTATION FOR DETAILS.                   
                                   22587                                                                                   
                                   22588                Note: This routine differs from the SCANSTR routine                
                                   22589                      above (which in my opinion has a bug). If you                
                                   22590                      scan a string whose very first character is                  
                                   22591                      in fact the stop character, then by the                      
                                   22592                      definition of the SYSCALL SCAN interfaces,                   
                                   22593                      you should get a NULL token. That doesn't                    
                                   22594                      happen with SCANSTR above, but too many people               
                                   22595                      have probably coded around that to change the                
                                   22596                      function of that routine. Thus, we introduce                 
                                   22597                      this routine, and additional SYSCALL XSCAN                   
                                   22598                      routines.                                                    
                                   22599                                                                                   
                                   22600                                                                                   
                                   22601                                                                                   
                                   22602

0                                  23064              *
                                   23065              *  XSCNTYPE - RETURN TYPE OF TOKEN, EXEC FILE VERSION.
                                   23066              *
                                   23067              *
                                   23068              *  ON ENTRY:
                                   23069              *    R1,R0 - TOKEN LOC, LEN
                                   23070              *  ON EXIT:
                                   23071              *    R1,R0 - TYPE LOC, LEN
                                   23072              *
                                   23073              *  NOTE:
                                   23074              *  THE ONLY TYPES RETURNED ARE:
                                   23075              *    NULL, ALPHA, NUMBER, AND OTHER
                                   23076              *  NULL IS END OF SCAN (IRRESPECTIVE OF ';'), ALPHA IS ALL
                                   23077              *  ALPHAS SCANNED, NUMBER IS ALL NUMBERS SCANNED.
                                   23078              *
                                   23079              *  NOTE2:
                                   23080              *  THIS IS JUNK.  IT WOULD HAVE BEEN BETTER FOR EXEC FILES
                                   23081              *  TO HAVE SEPARATE SCAN ROUTINES AND TYPE ROUTINES.
                                   23082              *  ONLY MINIMAL TYPING IS DONE HERE.  PERHAPS A SOMEDAY A
                                   23083              *  FEW TYPE PROCESSING SYSCALL WILL BE PROVIDED. WHATEVER.
                                   23084              *  WHENEVER.
                                   23085              *
                                   23086              *

0                                  27108              *
                                   27109              **
                                   27110              **  SCAN CHECK
                                   27111              **
                                   27112              **  ON ENTRY:
                                   27113              **       CPNSCANP - SCAN CONTROL BLOCK
                                   27114              **       R15 - RETURN COND FROM SCAN CALL
                                   27115              **
                                   27116              **  IF R15 IS A NEGATIVE RETURN CODE, WE PRINT THE ERROR
                                   27117              **  MESSAGE AND ABORT THE COMMAND.   IF R15 IS >= 0, WE
                                   27118              **  RETURN TO THE CALLER.
                                   27119              **
                                   27120              **  CAUTION:
                                   27121              **    IF R15 IS NEGATIVE, THIS ROUTINE WILL NOT RETURN.
                                   27122              **
                                   27123              **  CAUTION:
                                   27124              **    DO NOT CALL SCANCHK FROM WITHIN SCAN MODULE. IT USES
                                   27125              **    CPNSCANP POINTER.
                                   27126              **
                                   27127              **  NOTE:
                                   27128              **    CPNSCANP MUST POINT TO SCAN CONTROL BLOCK.  THIS
                                   27129              **    MAY NOT BE THE CASE DURING INITIALIZATION.  WE DO
                                   27130              **    NOT PASS SCAN CB IN R0 OR R1, BECAUSE THOSE ARE
                                   27131              **    SET WITH SCAN RETURNS THAT WE DO NOT WANT TO DIDDLE.
                                   27132              **    IT WOULD BE NICE NOT TO HAVE TO MAKE THIS ASSUMPTION
                                   27133              **    AND USE THE SCCBADR MACRO OF THE CALLER... BUT THIS
                                   27134              **    IS NOT POSSIBLE HERE.  (SCCBADR IS DIFFERENT IN SCAN
                                   27135              **    MODULE).   OH WELL FOR NOW.
                                   27136              *

                                   27898              **  THIS ROUTINE WILL UPPER CASE TOKEN AND PUT
